مقدمة الناشر
٣١
الرد على منطق اليونان). وقد أردتُ تلخيصه في كراريس قليلة تقريباً على الطلاب، وتسهيلاً على أولي الألباب فشرعت في ذلك وسميته «جَهْد القريحة في تجريد النصيحة، والله الهادي للصواب وقال في آخره: «هذا آخر ما لخصته من كتاب ابن تيمية. وقد أوردتُ عبارته بلفظه من غير تصرف في الغالب، وحذفت من كتابه الكثير فإنه في عشرين كراساً، ولم أحذف من المهم شيئاً. إنما حذفت ما لا تعلق له بالمقصود مما ذكر استطراداً، أو ردّاً على مسائل من إلهيات ونحوها، أو مكرراً، أو نقضاً لعباراتِ بعض المناطقة وليس راجعاً لقاعدة كلية في الفن أو نحو ذلك .
وقد طبع هذا المختصر مع كتاب صَوْن المنطق والكلام عن فن المنطق والكلام للسيوطي بمصر سنة ١٣٦٦ هـ ، بتصحيح الأستاذ على سامي النشار، صفحاته ١٤٣ ، بالقطع المتوسط. طُبع عن نسخة خطية في مكتبة الأزهر سقيمة، وقابلنا نسختنا عليها فألفيناها مشحونة بالأغلاط، غير أننا قد استفدنا منها في تصحيح بعض الأغلاط الموجودة في نسختنا، ورمزنا إليها بـ (س) . وبالتالي سيجد مصححه الفاضل في طبعتنا هذه خيرَ عَوْنٍ على تصحيح المختصر عند إعادة طبعه .
مساعدة
ما زالت أمنيتنا طبع هذا الكتاب الفذ منذ عرفنا النسخة الآصفية قبل أكثر من عشرين سنة، إلى أن جاء الله تعالى بحضرة صاحب المعالي وزير مالية المملكة العربية السعودية
السعودية، الشيخ عبد الله بن سليمان الحَمْدان - أطال الله عمره في صالح الأعمال ـ إلى بمباي سنة ١٣٦٢ هـ . فتبرع بالاشتراك في طبعه معنا لحكومة صاحب الجلالة السعودية ومحيي السنة المحمدية، الإمام عبد العزيز آل سعود ملك المملكة العربية السعودية - أيد الله تعالى به العلم والدين وأعز بسيفه الإسلام والمسلمين. فجعل الله ذلك سبباً لطبعه على أيدينا فالحمد لله الذي هدانا لهذا وما كنا لنهتدي لولا أن هدانا الله . ربنا ! تقبل منا ، إنك أنت السميع العليم.
الحكومة
بالجميل
ونشكر كل من ساعدنا على نشر هذا الكتاب، لا سيما عَمَلة دائرة المعارف اعتراف العثمانية، وبالأخص ناظمها الحالي حضرة الدكتور محمد نظام الدين حيث لم يألُ جَهْداً في تيسير أسباب الاستفادة عن النسخة الخطية والمكتبة الآصفية ومديرها حضرة
٣٢
نسخة
مقدمة الناشر
الدكتور محمد راحة الله خان إذ سمح لنا الاستفادة عن نسختها النادرة الوجود وأخذ الصور الشمسية عنها ومحب العلم والعلماء العالم السلفي الكريم الشيخ محمد نصيف من أعيان جُدّة (الحجاز ) إذ له سابق الفضل في حثّ دائرة المعارف العثمانية لإعطائنا من الكتاب ومؤازرتنا التامة أثناء طبعه وصاحب الفضل والكرم عالم المعقول والمنقول حضرة الأستاذ الأكبر السيد أحمد أبو الكلام آزاد حيث كتب لنا وصية رسمية من قبل حكومة الهند إلى أرباب السلطة بحيدر آباد لمساعدتنا حين سَفَرنا إلى تلك الديار ، فجزاهم الله كلهم أحسن الجزاء.
وأخيراً لا يسعني إلا الاعتراف بما قام به شقيقاي عبد الحكيم شرف الدين وخليل شرف الدين من أنواع المساعدات المادية والمعنوية التي لم يمكن طبع الكتاب بدونها، فكان سعيهما مشكوراً.
والحمد لله رب العالمين وصلى الله على سيدنا محمد خاتم النبيين .
دار القيمة»، إسلام آباد(بيمري)
بجوار بمباي (الهند)
۱۸ شوال ١٣٦٨ هـ، ١٤ أغسطس ١٩٤٩
عبد الصمد شرف الدين الكتبي النرول .
Publisher's Introduction
31
The Refutation of the Logic of the Greeks). I intended to summarize it in a few booklets for the students, and to facilitate for the intelligent, so I began that and named it 'Jahd al-Qariha fi Tajrid al-Nasiha', and God is the Guide to correctness. And he said at its end: 'This is the end of what I summarized from Ibn Taymiyya's book. I have presented his words verbatim without alteration for the most part, and I omitted much from his book, for it is in twenty booklets, and I omitted nothing of importance. I only omitted what is not related to the intended purpose, such as digressions, or refutations of matters of theology and the like, or repetitions, or criticisms of the expressions of some logicians that do not relate to a universal principle in the art or the like.' And this abridgment was printed with the book 'Sawn al-Mantiq wal-Kalam 'an Fann al-Mantiq wal-Kalam' by al-Suyuti in Egypt in the year 1366 AH, edited by Professor Ali Sami al-Nashar, 143 pages, medium size. It was printed from a defective manuscript in the Azhar Library, and we compared our copy with it and found it full of errors, but we benefited from it in correcting some errors in our copy, and we denoted it by (S). Hence, the honorable corrector in our edition will find a good aid for correcting the abridgment when reprinting it.
Assistance
Our desire to print this unique book remained since we knew the Asafiyya manuscript more than twenty years ago, until Allah brought His Excellency the Minister of Finance of the Kingdom of Saudi Arabia, Sheikh Abdullah bin Sulaiman al-Hamdan - may Allah prolong his life in righteous deeds - to Bombay in 1362 AH. He kindly agreed to share the cost of printing it with us for the government of His Majesty the Saudi King and reviver of the Prophetic Sunnah, Imam Abdul Aziz Al Saud, King of the Kingdom of Saudi Arabia - may Allah support knowledge and religion through him and strengthen Islam and Muslims with his sword. So Allah made this a reason for its printing by our hands. Praise be to Allah who guided us to this, and we would not have been guided unless Allah guided us. Our Lord! Accept from us, indeed You are the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.
Gratitude to the Government
And we thank everyone who helped us in publishing this book, especially the workers of the Ottoman Encyclopedia, and particularly its current director, His Excellency Dr. Muhammad Nizam al-Din, who spared no effort in facilitating the means of benefiting from the manuscript and the Asafiyya Library, and its director, His Excellency Dr. Muhammad Rahatullah Khan, who allowed us to benefit from its rare copy and take photographs of it. And the lover of knowledge and scholars, the noble Salafi scholar Sheikh Muhammad Nasif, a notable from Jeddah (Hijaz), who had prior merit in urging the Ottoman Encyclopedia to give us the book and his full support during its printing. And the possessor of virtue and generosity, the great scholar of rational and transmitted sciences, His Excellency the Senior Professor Sayyid Ahmad Abu al-Kalam Azad, who wrote an official recommendation from the Indian government to the authorities in Hyderabad to assist us during our travel to those lands. May Allah reward them all with the best reward.
Finally, I must acknowledge the various material and moral assistances provided by my two brothers, Abdul Hakim Sharaf al-Din and Khalil Sharaf al-Din, without which the printing of this book would not have been possible. Their efforts are appreciated.
Praise be to Allah, Lord of the worlds, and blessings upon our master Muhammad, the Seal of the Prophets.
Dar al-Qima, Islamabad (Bimri)
Near Bombay (India)
18 Shawwal 1368 AH, 14 August 1949
Abd al-Samad Sharaf al-Din al-Kutubi al-Narul.
Source pages p. 31

Commentary
This passage is the publisher's introduction to the edition of Ibn Taymiyya's 'Radd 'ala al-Mantiqiyyin'. The publisher, Abd al-Samad Sharaf al-Din, explains that he abridged Ibn Taymiyya's lengthy work into a concise treatise for students, preserving the original wording and only omitting digressions. He then recounts the history of the manuscript, noting a previous defective edition, and expresses gratitude to various benefactors who facilitated the printing, including Saudi officials, Indian scholars, and his own brothers. The introduction provides context about the importance of the work and the collaborative effort behind this edition. The passage contains no logical argument but documents the editorial process and acknowledges support.

Key Terms
التلخيص (talkhis): The act of summarizing Ibn Taymiyya's book into a shorter version for students. [Note: In classical works, talkhis often refers to summarizing a larger text while retaining key content.]
النسخة الآصفية (al-nuskha al-asafiyya): A specific manuscript copy of the work kept in the Asafiyya Library.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the publisher, what was the primary reason for omitting parts of Ibn Taymiyya's original text?
A) They were too difficult for students.
B) They were not related to the main purpose, like digressions or repetitions.
C) They were considered heretical.
D) The publisher had limited space.

Key Takeaway
The publisher's introduction teaches us that abridgment is a deliberate scholarly act that preserves core content while omitting extraneous material, and that textual transmission involves collaborative patronage.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
Compare the publisher's criteria for omission in this introduction with the criteria used by a hadith scholar when selecting a hadith for a collection. What similarities do you notice?
?
Write a short paragraph explaining why it matters that the publisher preserved Ibn Taymiyya's wording 'verbatim for the most part'. How does this affect our trust in the abridgment?

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
5 min
The Chain of Transmission of Ibn Taymiyya's Radd al-Mantiqiyyin
Publisher thanks contributors and describes manuscript source.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to reconstruct the network of individuals who facilitated the publication of Ibn Taymiyya's Radd al-Mantiqiyyin and explain the significance of each contribution.

Core Idea
A book's journey to print reveals the collective effort of scholars across generations.

This lesson examines the publisher's preface of Ibn Taymiyya's Radd al-Mantiqiyyin. Though it contains no logical arguments, this front matter is a window into the scholarly chains of transmission and patronage that preserved and revived this important critique of Aristotelian logic. By analyzing the acknowledgments, we learn how one critical text reached modern readers.

Guided Path
1
Identify the publisher and his collaborators
Find the names of individuals thanked in the preface. What roles did they play in the publication?
2
Analyze the type of assistance
Categorize each person's contribution: access to manuscript, moral support, official letters, or printing support.
3
Map the geographical network
Where are the contributors from? Consider locations like India, Hyderabad, Jeddah. How does this reflect the spread of knowledge?
4
Assess the importance of each contribution
Which contribution was most critical for the publication? Why?

Publisher's Preface
Dr. Muhammad Raha'at Allah Khan who allowed us to benefit from the rare copy of it and take photographic reproductions of it, and the lover of knowledge and scholars, the virtuous Salafi scholar, Sheikh Muhammad Nasif, from the notables of Jeddah (Hijaz), as he had prior virtue in urging the Ottoman Encyclopedia to give us from the book and his full support during its printing, and the possessor of virtue and generosity, the scholar of rational and transmitted sciences, His Excellency the Great Teacher, Sayyid Ahmad Abu al-Kalam Azad, who wrote for us an official testament from the Indian government to the authorities in Hyderabad to assist us during our travel to that land. May Allah reward them all with the best reward.
Finally, I cannot but acknowledge what my two brothers, Abd al-Hakim Sharaf al-Din and Khalil Sharaf al-Din, have done in terms of material and moral assistance, without which the printing of the book would not have been possible. Their effort is appreciated.
Praise be to Allah, Lord of the worlds, and blessings be upon our master Muhammad, the seal of the prophets.
Dar al-Qayyimah, Islamabad (Bimri)
Near Bombay (India)

Abd al-Samad Sharaf al-Din al-Kutubi al-Narul.
The heavens and the earth suffice us from evil.

Commentary
This passage is the publisher's preface. It thanks individuals who helped in obtaining the manuscript and publishing the book. The author of the preface is Abd al-Samad Sharaf al-Din. He acknowledges Dr. Muhammad Raha'at Allah Khan for allowing access to the rare copy, Sheikh Muhammad Nasif for his encouragement, and Maulana Abul Kalam Azad for an official testament from the Indian government. He also thanks his two brothers for their material and moral assistance. The preface ends with publication details and a note about the manuscript cover image, explaining that the image is unclear due to wear. This passage provides context for the edition but does not contain logical content.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner

Parsing a Classical Book Title Page
Title page with author and editorial metadata.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to extract the author's name, dates, and editorial chain from a classical Islamic book title page.

Core Idea
The title page is a scholarly chain of transmission.

When you open a classical Islamic text, the title page often contains crucial information about authorship, date, and the manuscript's editorial journey. This lesson will teach you how to parse such a title page using the example of Ibn Taymiyya's 'al-Radd 'ala al-Mantiqiyyin'.

Guided Path
1
Identify the Title(s)
Look for the main title and any alternate titles. Here, the main title is 'al-Radd 'ala al-Mantiqiyyin' and an alternate is 'Nasihat Ahl al-Iman fi Radd Mantiq al-Yunan'.
Alternate titles often clarify the book's content.
2
Extract Author's Full Name and Dates
Find the author's full genealogical name and birth/death (or lifespan) dates. Here: 'Taqi al-Din Abu al-Abbas Ahmad ibn Abd al-Halim Ibn Taymiyya', born 661 H, died 728 H.
The name often includes honorifics and lineage.
3
Identify Editors and Other Contributors
Note any names of those who presented, verified, or prepared the edition. Here: a presenter (al-Kirli?man al-Badawi?) and editors/verifiers (Abd al-Samad Sharaf al-Din al-Kabbi?, Muhammad Talha Bilal Munyar).
Editors' credentials and dates help assess the edition's reliability.
4
Evaluate the Scholarly Chain
Assess whether the contributors are known scholars. The garbled names suggest possible OCR errors; critical reading requires cross-checking with reliable sources.
A clear scholarly chain adds authority to the edition.

Source Text

كتاب الرد على المنطقيين المسمى أيضا نَصيحة أهل الإيمان في الرد على منطق اليونان للإمام الحمام شيخ الإسلام العلامة تقي الدين أبي العباس أحمد بن عبد الحليم ابن تيمية العراقي المولود سنة ٦٦١ هـ والمتوفى سنة ٧٢٨ هـ رحمة الله تعالى قدم له العلامة التركتور الكيرليمان التدوي المتوفى سنة ١٣٧٣هـ مدير مجلة "معارف والقاضي بالمحكمة الشرعية بيوفال حققه راجعة واعدة لهذه الطبيعة الشيخ عبد الصمد شرف الدين الكبيي محمد طلحة بلال منيار رحمة الله تعالى
The book The Refutation of the Logicians, also titled Advice to the People of Faith in Refuting the Logic of the Greeks, by the Imam, the protector, the Shaykh of Islam, the scholar Taqi al-Din Abu al-Abbas Ahmad ibn Abd al-Halim Ibn Taymiyya al-Iraqi, born in the year 661 H and died in the year 728 H, may God have mercy on him. Presented by the scholar, the doctor, al-Kirli?man al-Badawi?, died in the year 1373 H, director of the journal "Ma'arif" and judge at the Shari'a court in Yufal? Verified, reviewed, and prepared for this edition by Shaykh Abd al-Samad Sharaf al-Din al-Kabbi? Muhammad Talha Bilal Munyar, may God have mercy on them.
Source pages p. 42

Commentary
This passage is the title page of Ibn Taymiyya's work 'The Refutation of the Logicians' (al-Radd 'ala al-Mantiqiyyin). It gives the full title, the author's name and biographical details (birth 661 AH, death 728 AH), and information about the editors of this edition. The title page also mentions an alternate title and lists a preface writer and two editors/verifiers. The text is typical of a manuscript title page, and the student should note the precise identification of the author and his dates to situate the work historically. The garbled names (e.g., "الكيرليمان" and "بيوفال") are likely OCR errors for known scholars, but their exact forms are uncertain.

Key Terms
المنطقيين (al-mantiqiyyin): Logicians, specifically those of the Greek/Peripatetic tradition whom Ibn Taymiyya refutes. [Note: Stable term referring to practitioners of Greek logic.]

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint

Key Takeaway
A classical book title page is a scholarly chain that identifies the author, his dates, and the editorial history of the text.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?

?
Why is it important to know the death date of the person who 'presented' or 'verified' the edition? Explain using the example from this lesson.
